obſeruationē ex ea autoritate deſcendere ꝙ poſt aſcenſum dn̄i ſpūs ſanctꝰ ad apoſtolos deſcēdit et multis ī locis idem factitatū reperimus ad honorē potius ſacerdotij quam legis neceſsitatē alioqui ſi ad epiſcopi tātùm imprecationē ſpūs ſanctꝰ defluit lugēdi ſunt qui viculis aut caſtellis aut ī remotioribus locis per praeſbyteros diaconos baptizati antè dormierunt quàm ab epiſcopis ſcriptures knowledge pope ſeuen hundreth yeres beleue therefore lette poin • te ſhe may head whole churche well rather pope ſhée ſit publique iudgement determine controuerſies dooe hir iuſtices general armie noble hir ſubiectes ſaye ſhée • execute ciuill office hir owne perſon would therfore dorman take hir hir ciuill principalitie ouer hir ſubiectes ſhe ſhall prince head vnder god surely may good reaſon dooe woulde take away hir ſuperioritie ouer hir clergie hir ſhe may execute eccleſiaſticall function though quéenes maieſtie haue vnderſtanding affaire hir realme experience thinges
